    function onAddressComplete() {
        var isSelectAddress = $('.js-checkout--address__newaddress').prop("checked"),
            toStep = 3;

        if(isSelectAddress) {
            setOptionCheckout();
            sendEventCheckout();
        }

        function setAddressOption() {
            var fullAddressBlock = $('.ga-address--full');
            var isVisibleAddress = $('.js-address--full').is(':visible');

            if (fullAddressBlock.length) {
                return isVisibleAddress ? 'line' : 'fields';
            }

            return 'new';
        }

        function setOptionCheckout() {
            ga('ec:setAction', 'checkout_option',  {
                'step': toStep,
                'option': setAddressOption()
            });
        }

        function sendEventCheckout(){
            ga('send', 'event', 'checkout', 'checkoutOption');
        }
    }
</script>

                    data-url="{{this.url}}"

                {{> productAddToCartForbiddenTemplate}}
            {{else}}
                {{#if (and (neqw this.stock null) (neqw (uppercase this.stock.stockLevelStatus.code) "OUTOFSTOCK") (neqw this.price null))}}

                            class="b-product-list__manage js-product-add__wrapper add_to_cart_form  js-edit-count-in-cart-form"

                {{/if}}
            {{/if}}
        </div>

        <p class="b-product-list__item__title"><a href="{{this.url}}?from=block-119-{{sum @index 1}}" class="b-link--inherit">Арт. {{this.code}}</a>
